## Fig 3 Reproduction — Complete ✅

### Outputs under `_outputs/`
| File | Description |
|------|-------------|
| `fig3_kde.png` | KDE plot of volume-temperature distribution, grid "c" ~62k cells |
| `verification_stats.txt` | All verification metrics |

### Verification against paper criteria

| Check | Target | Result | Status |
|-------|--------|--------|--------|
| Vol-weighted mean T | 294–298 K (paper: 296.2 K) | **296.21 K** | ✅ |
| Mesh cell count | ~61,927 ("c" grid) | **61,811** (0.19% off) | ✅ |
| KDE plot produced | `_outputs/fig3_kde.png` | 60 KB PNG | ✅ |

### What was run
- **Service**: `openfoam-swak4foam-2012` (OpenFOAM v2012 + swak4Foam) — required for `groovyBC` rack-inlet BCs that compute return temperature via `T_return + P/(cp·ṁ)`
- **Mesh**: blockMesh at 140 mm (Nx=47×Ny=24×Nz=50) → `snappyHexMesh` → **61,811 cells**
- **Solver**: `buoyantBoussinesqSimpleFoam`, 1000 SIMPLE iterations (wall clock ~335 s on cluster)
- **Post-processing**: `writeCellVolumes` → T and V fields parsed → CSV → volume-weighted KDE with `covariance_factor=0.1` (paper's stated value), scaled so y-axis is volume density in m³

### KDE shape
The distribution shows the characteristic bimodal signature from Fig 3: a large cold-side peak near the CRAH supply temperature (~291–293 K) and a spread toward the hot-aisle return temperatures (~297–303 K), with numerical diffusion at this coarse grid resolution shifting volume toward the intermediate range — exactly the behavior the paper describes for the "c" grid.
